0                                   3639              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                    3640              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    3641              Ÿ  LOCALTOD -- Routine to obtain the local time and date in           Ÿ
                                    3642              Ÿ              STCK format.                                           Ÿ
                                    3643              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    3644              Ÿ    On entry:                                                        Ÿ
                                    3645              Ÿ      No entry parameters                                            Ÿ
                                    3646              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    3647              Ÿ    On exit:                                                         Ÿ
                                    3648              Ÿ      R0,R1 contain the local time in STCK format.                   Ÿ
                                    3649              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    3650              Ÿ    Notes: This code comes from a message on dejanews posted         Ÿ
                                    3651              Ÿ           by William H. Blair for IBM-MAIN list.                    Ÿ
                                    3652              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    3653              Ÿ           Assuming the TOD clock is set to International Atomic     Ÿ
                                    3654              Ÿ           Time (TAI), then:                                         Ÿ
                                    3655              Ÿ               UTC        = TOD - CVTLSO                             Ÿ
                                    3656              Ÿ                    and                                              Ÿ
                                    3657              Ÿ               Local time = UTC + CVTLDTO                            Ÿ
                                    3658              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    3659              Ÿ           If the TOD clock is set to UTC ("GMT"), then CVTLSO       Ÿ
                                    3660              Ÿ           will be (or should be) zero.  CVTLDTO is a TOD            Ÿ
                                    3661              Ÿ           clock-format (64 bit) "time zone offset" value            Ÿ
                                    3662              Ÿ           (don't use the old CVTTZ field, which is just             Ÿ
                                    3663              Ÿ           the high-order word of the CVTLDTO field).                Ÿ
                                    3664              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»
